This may have been a result of me incorrectly\n            # using the upstream library, or an upstream bug. this is the key test for the bug\n5. **Confirms the engine is still usable** by checking `_engine is not None`\n\n### Why This Tests the Bug\n\nThe bug occurs when:\n- The app tries to deserialize a corrupted cache file\n- A `DeserializationError` is raised by the adblock library\n- **The exception is not properly caught**, causing the app to crash during initialization\n\nThe test demonstrates that the fix works correctly by:\n- Confirming the exception is **caught and handled gracefully**\n- Confirming an **error message is displayed** (via the exception handler)\n- Confirming the **app continues running** with the engine in a usable state\n\n### Running the Test\n\nThe test can be run with:\n```bash\npython3 -m pytest -c /dev/null --timeout=60 /workspace/regression_test.py -v\n```\n\nOr without the timeout flag if pytest-timeout is not available:\n```bash\npython3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py -v\n```","stop_reason":null,"session_id":"4d844f7b-6ff9-40cb-a7b4-386af3b65cb0","total_cost_usd":0.7123149499999998,"usage":{"input_tokens":400,"cache_creation_input_tokens":79717,"cache_read_input_tokens":4492737,"output_tokens":32599,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":79717,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"},"modelUsage":{"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001":{"inputTokens":400,"outputTokens":32599,"cacheReadInputTokens":4492737,"cacheCreationInputTokens":79717,"webSearchRequests":0,"costUSD":0.7123149499999998,"contextWindow":200000,"maxOutputTokens":32000}},"permission_denials":[],"fast_mode_state":"off","uuid":"f45afea6-9636-4066-84ad-feac0d480ee3"}
